# <a name="obsolete-members-in-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="74c0d-105">.NET Framework eski Üyeler</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="74c0d-105">Obsolete members in .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="74c0d-106">Bu makalede .NET Framework 4,5 ve sonraki sürümlerde kullanılmayan tür üyeleri listelenmektedir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="74c0d-106">This article list the type members that are obsolete in .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="74c0d-107">Tür üyeleri derlemeye göre gruplandırılır.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="74c0d-107">Type members are grouped by assembly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="74c0d-108">Bu makale, eski türlerin üyelerini listeetmez.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="74c0d-108">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="74c0d-109">Eski türlerin listesi için bkz. [Eski türler](obsolete-types.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="74c0d-109">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>
